Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

017521,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 210.
017522,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
017523,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 15-17.
017524,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
017525,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
017526,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017527,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
017528,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 402-486

017541,000024:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017542,000025:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017543,000026:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017544,000027:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017545,000028: 
017546,000029:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017547,000030: 
017548,000031:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017549,000032:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017550,000033:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017551,000034:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017552,000035:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017553,000036:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017554,000037:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017555,000038:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017556,000039:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017557,000040: 
017558,000041:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017559,000042:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017560,000043:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017561,000044:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017562,000045:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017563,000046:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017564,000047: 
017565,000048: 
017566,000049:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017567,000050: 
017568,000051:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017569,000052:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017570,000053:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017571,000054:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017572,000055:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017573,000056: 
017574,000057:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017575,000058:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017576,000059:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017577,000060:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017578,000061: 
017579,000062:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017580,000063:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017581,000064:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017582,000065:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017583,000066:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017584,000067: 
017585,000068: 
017586,000069:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
017587,000070: 
017588,000071:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017589,000072:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017590,000073:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 403 

017592,000075:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017593,000076:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017594,000077:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017595,000078:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017596,000079:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017597,000080:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017598,000081:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017599,000082:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017600,000083:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017601,000084:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017602,000085: 
017603,000086:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017604,000087:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017605,000088:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017606,000089: 
017607,000090: 
017608,000091:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017609,000092: 
017610,000093:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017611,000094:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017612,000095:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017613,000096: 
017614,000097:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017615,000098:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017616,000099:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017617,000100:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017618,000101:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017619,000102:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017620,000103:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017621,000104: 
017622,000105:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017623,000106:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017624,000107: 
017625,000108: 
017626,000109:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017627,000110: 
017628,000111:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017629,000112:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017630,000113:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017631,000114:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017632,000115: 
017633,000116: 
017634,000117:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017635,000118: 
017636,000119:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017637,000120:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017638,000121:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017639,000122:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017640,000123: 
017641,000124:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 404 

017643,000126:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017644,000127: 
017645,000128: 
017646,000129:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017647,000130: 
017648,000131:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017649,000132:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017650,000133: 
017651,000134:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017652,000135:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017653,000136:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017654,000137:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017655,000138: 
017656,000139:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017657,000140:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017658,000141: 
017659,000142:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017660,000143:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017661,000144:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017662,000145:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017663,000146: 
017664,000147:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017665,000148:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017666,000149: 
017667,000150:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017668,000151:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017669,000152: 
017670,000153:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017671,000154: 
017672,000155:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017673,000156:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017674,000157:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017675,000158:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017676,000159: 
017677,000160:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017678,000161:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017679,000162: 
017680,000163:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017681,000164:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017682,000165: 
017683,000166: 
017684,000167:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017685,000168:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017686,000169:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://www.ibiblio.org/apollo/hrst/archive/1706.pdf --- MAS 11/2016.)

017692,000175:

017694,000177:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

017696,000179:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
017697,000180: 
017698,000181:                                                                                                  #                       HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
017699,000182: 
017700,000183: 
017701,000184:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
017702,000185: 
017703,000186: 
017704,000187:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017705,000188: 
017706,000189:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017707,000190:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017708,000191:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017709,000192:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017710,000193:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017711,000194:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017712,000195:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017713,000196:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017714,000197:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017715,000198:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017716,000199:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017717,000200:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017718,000201:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017719,000202:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017720,000203:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017721,000204:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017722,000205:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017723,000206:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017724,000207:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017725,000208:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017726,000209:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017727,000210:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017728,000211:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
017729,000212:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017730,000213:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017731,000214:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017732,000215:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017733,000216:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017734,000217:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017735,000218:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017736,000219:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017737,000220:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017738,000221:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017739,000222:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017740,000223:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017741,000224:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017742,000225: 
017743,000226: 
017744,000227:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

Page 406 

017746,000229:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
017747,000230:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
017748,000231:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
017749,000232: 
017750,000233:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
017751,000234:                                                                                                  #  WDRET    =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
017752,000235:                                                                                                  #  DECRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
017753,000236:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG =      INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
017754,000237: 
017755,000238:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET =      POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
017756,000239:                                                                                                  #  CHAR     =      POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
017757,000240:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT    =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
017758,000241:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT  =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
017759,000242: 
017760,000243:                                                                                                  #  SGNON    =      VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
017761,000244:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM  =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
017762,000245:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
017763,000246:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
017764,000247: 
017765,000248:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
017766,000249:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017767,000250:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017768,000251:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017769,000252:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
017770,000253:                                                                                                  #  CODE     =      VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
017771,000254:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
017772,000255:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN  =      VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017773,000256:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.
017774,000257:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP  =      VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
017775,000258:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017776,000259: 
017777,000260:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
017778,000261: 
017779,000262:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET   =      DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
017780,000263: 
017781,000264:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT    =      DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
017782,000265:                                                                                                  #  INREL    =      DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR ( X,Y,Z, REG )
017783,000266: 
017784,000267:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM =      MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
017785,000268:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR    =      MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
017786,000269: 
017787,000270:                                                                                                  #  TEM1     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017788,000271:                                                                                                  #  DSREL    =      TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
017789,000272: 
017790,000273:                                                                                                  #  TEM2     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017791,000274:                                                                                                  #  DSMAG    =      TEM2            MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
017792,000275:                                                                                                  #  IDADDTEM =      TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
017793,000276: 
017794,000277:                                                                                                  #  TEM3     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017795,000278:                                                                                                  #  COUNT    =      TEM3            FOR DSPIN
017796,000279:

017798,000281:                                                                                                  #  TEM4     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017799,000282:                                                                                                  #  LSTPTR   =      TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
017800,000283:                                                                                                  #  RELRET   =      TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
017801,000284:                                                                                                  #  FREERET  =      TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
017802,000285:                                                                                                  #  DSPWDRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
017803,000286:                                                                                                  #  SEPSCRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
017804,000287:                                                                                                  #  SEPMNRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
017805,000288: 
017806,000289:                                                                                                  #  TEM5     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017807,000290:                                                                                                  #  NOUNADD  =      TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
017808,000291: 
017809,000292:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM  ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
017810,000293:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
017811,000294:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017812,000295:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, - IDAD3TEM-2.
017813,000296:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017814,000297:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, - IDAD3TEM-1.
017815,000298:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017816,000299:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.

017818,000301:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017819,000302:

017829,000312:

017847,000330:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
017848,000331:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
017849,000332:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
017850,000333:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
017851,000334:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
017852,000335:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
017853,000336:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
017854,000337:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
017855,000338:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
017856,000339:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
017857,000340:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
017858,000341:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

(003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017860,000343: 
017861,000344: 
017862,000345:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017863,000346:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017864,000347:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017865,000348:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017866,000349:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017867,000350:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017868,000351: 
017869,000352:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017870,000353:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017871,000354:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017872,000355:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017873,000356:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017874,000357:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017875,000358: 
017876,000359:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017877,000360:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1    11       ALL ARE OCTAL
017878,000361:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2    10
017879,000362:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3    7
017880,000363:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4    6
017881,000364:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5    5
017882,000365:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1    4
017883,000366:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2    3
017884,000367:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3    2
017885,000368:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4    1
017886,000369:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5    0
017887,000370:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017888,000371: 
017889,000372: 
017890,000373:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017891,000374: 
017892,000375:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017893,000376:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017894,000377:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017895,000378:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017896,000379:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017897,000380:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 409 

017899,000382:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017900,000383:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017901,000384:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017902,000385:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017903,000386:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017904,000387:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017905,000388:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017906,000389:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017907,000390: 
017908,000391: 
017909,000392:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017910,000393:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017911,000394:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017912,000395:                                                                                                  #  1          00011

017918,000401:                                                                                                  #  7          10011

018641,001124: 41,2401           61447                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
018642,001125:

Page 426 

018644,001127:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018645,001128:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018646,001129:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018647,001130:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018648,001131:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018649,001132:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018650,001133: 
018651,001134:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018652,001135:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018653,001136: 
018654,001137:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018655,001138: 
018656,001139:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018657,001140:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018658,001141:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018659,001142: 
018660,001143:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018661,001144:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018662,001145:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018663,001146:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018664,001147:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018665,001148:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018666,001149: 
018667,001150:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018668,001151:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018669,001152:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018670,001153:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018671,001154:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018672,001155: 
018673,001156:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018674,001157:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018675,001158:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018676,001159:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018677,001160:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018678,001161:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018679,001162:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018680,001163:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018681,001164: 
018682,001165: 
018683,001166:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018684,001167:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018685,001168:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018686,001169: 
018687,001170: 
018688,001171:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018689,001172:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018690,001173: 
018691,001174:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018692,001175:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018693,001176:

Page 427 

018695,001178:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018696,001179: 41,2402           44743        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018697,001180: 41,2403           02453                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018698,001181: 41,2404           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD

019908,002391:

Page 452 

019910,002393:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019911,002394:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019912,002395:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019913,002396:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019914,002397:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019915,002398: 
019916,002399:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019917,002400:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019918,002401:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019919,002402:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019920,002403:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019921,002404:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019922,002405:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019923,002406: 
019924,002407:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019925,002408:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019926,002409:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019927,002410: 
019928,002411:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019929,002412:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019930,002413: 
019931,002414:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019932,002415:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019933,002416: 
019934,002417:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
019935,002418: 41,3302                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN                              
019936,002419: 
019937,002420: 41,3302                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019938,002421: 41,3302           43311        MONITOR            CS       BIT15/14                              
019939,002422: 41,3303           71016                           MASK     NOUNCADR                              
019940,002423: 41,3304           54155        MONIT1             TS       MPAC       +1                         #  TEMP STORAGE
019941,002424: 41,3305           40136                           CS       ENTEXIT                               
019942,002425: 41,3306           64210                           AD       ENDINST

020062,002545:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
020063,002546:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
020064,002547:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
020065,002548: 
020066,002549:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
020067,002550: 
020068,002551:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
020069,002552:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
020070,002553:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
020071,002554: 
020072,002555:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
020073,002556:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
020074,002557:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
020075,002558: 
020076,002559: 41,3425           34310        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
020077,002560: 41,3426           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
020078,002561: 41,3427           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
020079,002562: 41,3430           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
020080,002563: 41,3431           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
020081,002564: 41,3432           04642                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
020082,002565: 41,3433           03435                           TC       DSPOCTWO

020513,002996:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
020514,002997:

Page 465 

020516,002999:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020517,003000: 
020518,003001:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020519,003002: 
020520,003003:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020521,003004:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020522,003005:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020523,003006:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020524,003007: 
020525,003008:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020526,003009:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020527,003010:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020528,003011: 
020529,003012:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020530,003013:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020531,003014:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020532,003015:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020533,003016:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020534,003017:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020535,003018:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020536,003019:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020537,003020:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020538,003021:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020539,003022:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020540,003023: 
020541,003024: 40,3517           44742        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020542,003025: 40,3520           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020543,003026: 40,3521           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020544,003027: 40,3522           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020545,003028: 40,3523           34727                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020546,003029: 40,3524           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020547,003030: 40,3525           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020548,003031: 40,3526           03535                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020549,003032: 40,3527           04450        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020550,003033: 40,3530           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020551,003034: 40,3531           03533                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020552,003035: 40,3532           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020553,003036: 40,3533           04626                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020554,003037: 40,3534           21062                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020555,003038: 40,3535           34746        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020556,003039: 40,3536           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020557,003040: 40,3537           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020558,003041: 40,3540           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020559,003042: 40,3541           04473                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020560,003043: 40,3542           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020561,003044: 
020562,003045: 40,3543                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020563,003046:

Page 466 

020565,003048:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020566,003049:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020567,003050:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020568,003051:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020569,003052:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020570,003053: 
020571,003054:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020572,003055:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020573,003056:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020574,003057: 
020575,003058:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020576,003059:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020577,003060: 
020578,003061:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020579,003062:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020580,003063:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020581,003064:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020582,003065:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020583,003066: 
020584,003067:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020585,003068:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020586,003069:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020587,003070:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020588,003071: 
020589,003072:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020590,003073:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020591,003074:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020592,003075:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020593,003076:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020594,003077:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020595,003078:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020596,003079: 
020597,003080:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020598,003081:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020599,003082: 
020600,003083:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020601,003084:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020602,003085: 
020603,003086:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020604,003087:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020605,003088: 
020606,003089:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020607,003090:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020608,003091:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020609,003092:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020610,003093:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020611,003094:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020612,003095:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020613,003096: 
020614,003097:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 467 

020616,003099:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020617,003100:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020618,003101:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020619,003102:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020620,003103:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020621,003104:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020622,003105:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020623,003106:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020624,003107:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020625,003108: 
020626,003109:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020627,003110:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020628,003111: 
020629,003112:    4145                                           SETLOC   MID7       +1                         
020630,003113:    4145                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020631,003114:    4145           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020632,003115:    4146           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP

020636,003119:    4152           10000                           CCS      A

020639,003122:    4155           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
020640,003123:    4156           55036                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
