020734,003217:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS ).
020735,003218: 
020736,003219:    4175                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
020737,003220:    4175                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020738,003221:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020739,003222:    4175           34726        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020740,003223:    4176           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020741,003224:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020742,003225:    4177           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020743,003226: 
020744,003227: 
020745,003228:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020746,003229:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020747,003230:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020748,003231:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020749,003232:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020750,003233: 
020751,003234: 
020752,003235:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020753,003236:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020754,003237:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020755,003238:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020756,003239:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020757,003240:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020758,003241:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020759,003242:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020760,003243:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020761,003244:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020762,003245: 
020763,003246: 
020764,003247:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
020765,003248:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020766,003249:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS

Page 470 

020768,003251:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020769,003252:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020770,003253:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020771,003254: 
020772,003255:    4200           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020773,003256:    4201           04211                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020774,003257:    4202           04215                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020775,003258:    4203           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020776,003259:    4204           75003                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020777,003260:    4205           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020778,003261:    4206           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020779,003262:    4207           05124                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020780,003263: 
020781,003264: 
020782,003265:    4210           05146        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020783,003266: 
020784,003267: 
020785,003268:    4211           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020786,003269:    4212           04220                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020827,003310: 
020828,003311: 
020829,003312:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
020830,003313:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
020831,003314:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
020832,003315:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
020833,003316: 
020834,003317:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT IS RESTORED TO STATE IT WAS IN BEFORE BLANKSUB WAS EXECUTED.
020835,003318: 
020836,003319:    4246           74750        BLANKSUB           MASK     SEVEN                                 
020837,003320:    4247           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                #  STORE BLANKING CODE IN NVTEMP.
020838,003321:    4250           34727                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020839,003322:    4251           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT

Page 478 

021123,003606:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021124,003607: 
021125,003608:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021126,003609:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021127,003610:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021128,003611:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021129,003612: 
021130,003613:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021131,003614:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021132,003615:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021133,003616:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021134,003617:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021135,003618:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021136,003619:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021137,003620: 
021138,003621: 
021139,003622:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021140,003623:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021141,003624:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021142,003625:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021143,003626:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021144,003627: 
021145,003628: 
021146,003629:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021147,003630:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021148,003631:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021149,003632:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021150,003633:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021151,003634: 
021152,003635: 
021153,003636:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021154,003637:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021155,003638:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021156,003639: 
021157,003640: 
021158,003641:                                                                                                  #  .
021159,003642: 
021160,003643: 
021161,003644:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021162,003645:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021163,003646:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL
021164,003647:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021165,003648: 
021166,003649: 
021167,003650:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021168,003651:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021169,003652:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021170,003653:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021171,003654:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021172,003655:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 479

021198,003681:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021199,003682:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021200,003683:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021201,003684:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
